Wow! My husband and I had one of the BEST customer service experiences at this Purchase Green, thanks to Alexandra and Israel! <resp>None< /resp><Time>1616729096516</Time><gmapID>0x808f914094fdfb0d:0xee9364d8ccb35c< /gmapID>< Review>
Food is okay, wish they had more variety for the $5.99 value duet special.

Sometimes the curbside pickup takes 10-15 minutes longer than your pickup time.

Bakery items are good, the orange scone, brownie, cinnamon bun, bear claw and chocolate croissant are my go to.

Portions are small and overpriced.

They do taste good though.

I‚Äôm recommending the:
Broccoli cheddar Mac and cheese
$5.99 tuna and soup
Turkey chili
Napa Chicken salad sandwich
Blood Orange Refresher

Tuesday Bagel special is good, I recommend getting the honey walnut cream cheese.

WiFi is good so if you want to eat in your car it covers the parking lot.</Review>
